NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

under the style of VVD Sales Management Services. And registered at Madras North, with the Registrar of Firms on
3rd February 2010 being No. B2/816/2010 has been dissolved as from the 1st day of October 2009. All debts, claims, etc.,
owing by and due to the said firm will be paid and received by VVD and Sons Private Limited who has been authorised by
all partners to give effectual receipts and discharges for all debts and claims due to the firm, and to do all such things as
may be necessary to wind up the affairs of the firm and to complete transactions begun but unfinished at the time of dissolution.
